PARAGRAPH_71839: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71840: 1. Compliance and reporting obligations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71841: Status of these guidelines

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71842: 1. This document contains guidelines issued pursuant to Article 16 of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010. 7 In accordance with Article 16(3) of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010, competent authorities and credit institutions must make every effort to comply with the guidelines.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71843: 2. Guidelines set out the EBA's view of appropriate supervisory practices within the European System of Financial Supervision or of how Union law should be applied in a particular area. Competent authorities as defined in Article 4(2) of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010 to which guidelines apply should comply by incorporating them into their practices as appropriate (e.g. by amending their legal framework or their supervisory processes), including where guidelines are directed primarily at institutions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71844: Reporting requirements

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71845: 3. In accordance with Article 16(3) of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010, competent authorities must notify the EBA that they comply or intend to comply with these guidelines, or otherwise give reasons for non-compliance, by ([dd.mm.yyyy]). In the absence of any notification by this deadline, competent authorities will be considered by the EBA to be non-compliant. Notifications should be sent by submitting the form available on the EBA website to compliance@eba.europa.eu with the reference 'EBA/GL/201x/xx'. Notifications should be submitted by persons with appropriate authority to report compliance on behalf of their competent authorities. Any change in the status of compliance must also be reported to the EBA.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71846: 4. Notifications will be published on the EBA website, in line with Article 16(3) of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:13]
PARAGRAPH_71847: 7 Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 24 November 2010 establishing a European Supervisory Authority (European Banking Authority), amending Decision No 716/2009/EC and repealing Commission Decision 2009/78/EC, (OJ L 331, 15.12.2010, p. 12).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71849: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71851: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71852: 2. Subject matter, scope and definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71853: Subject matter

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71854: 5. These guidelines specify sound risk management practices for credit institutions for managing non-performing exposures (NPEs), forborne exposures (FBEs) and foreclosed assets.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71855: 6. These guidelines also provide competent authorities with guidance on assessing credit institutions' risk management practices, policies, processes and procedures for managing NPEs and FBEs as part of the supervisory review and evaluation process (SREP).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71856: Scope of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71857: 7. These guidelines apply in relation to Article 74 of Directive 2013/36/EU,8 which requires institutions to have robust governance arrangements, including a clear organisational structure with well-defined, transparent and consistent lines of responsibility, effective processes to identify, manage, monitor and report the risks they are or might be exposed to and adequate control mechanisms.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71858: 8. Competent authorities should ensure that credit institutions comply with these guidelines on an individual, sub-consolidated and consolidated basis in accordance with Article 109 of Directive 2013/36/EU.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71859: 9. All sections of these guidelines apply to all exposures subject to definitions of non-performing and forbearance as defined in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014.9

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71860: 10.For the purposes of the abovementioned definitions of non-performing and forborne exposures in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014, trading exposures include the exposures in the trading book defined in point 86 of Article 4(1) of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71861: 11.Credit institutions with a gross NPL ratio equal to or greater than 5% on consolidated, sub- consolidated or solo level should apply sections 4 and 5 of these guidelines to the entities that have NPL ratios exceeding the set threshold.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71862: 8 Directive 2013/36/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council of 26 June 2013 on access to the activity of credit institutions and the prudential supervision of credit institutions and investment firms, amending Directive 2002/87/EC and repealing Directives 2006/48/EC and 2006/49/EC, (OJ L 176, 27.6.2013, p. 338).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:14]
PARAGRAPH_71863: 9 Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014 of 16 April 2014 laying down implementing technical standards with regard to supervisory reporting of institutions according to Regulation (EU) No 575/2013 of the European Parliament and of the Council, (OJ L 191, 28.6.2014, p. 1).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71865: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71867: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71868: 12. Where credit institutions have a gross NPL ratio below the 5% level but have a high share or material amount of NPEs in an individual portfolio or individual portfolios with a specific concentration of NPEs in a geographical region, an economic sector or a group of connected clients, competent authorities may require credit institutions to apply sections 4 and 5 at the level of these portfolios.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71869: 13.Furthermore, competent authorities may identify credit institutions other than those covered in paragraph 11 that should also apply sections 4 and 5. Competent authorities should require the application of these sections if they identify signs of deteriorating asset quality. Competent authorities should consider the following elements and their interactions when assessing the applicability of sections 4 and 5:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71870: a) increased inflows of NPEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71871: b) a high or increased level of FBEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71872: c) a high or increased level of foreclosed assets;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71873: d) low coverage ratios;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71874: e) breached early warning indicators;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71875: f) an elevated Texas ratio;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71876: g) the quality and appropriateness of workout activity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71877: 14.All credit institutions should apply sections 6 to 9.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71878: 15.Credit institutions should comply with these guidelines in a manner that is appropriate to their size and internal organisation and the nature, scope and complexity of their activities; in particular, credit institutions may comply with sections 4 and 5 taking into account the proportionality criteria specified in section 4, Title I, of the EBA Guidelines on internal governance.10 Furthermore, if the credit institution is classified by the competent authorities for SREP purposes as SREP Category 3 or 4 (as assigned in accordance with the EBA Guidelines on common procedures and methodologies for the SREP11), then the guidelines should be applied in a proportionate manner. The principle of proportionality in the application of these guidelines will relate in particular to simplified obligations for the operationalisation and governance arrangements supporting the NPE strategies of credit institutions (section 5).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71879: 10 Guidelines on internal governance under Directive 2013/36/EU (EBA/GL/2017/11).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:15]
PARAGRAPH_71880: 11 Described in section 2.1.1, 'Categorisation of institutions', of the Guidelines on common procedures and methodologies for the supervisory review and evaluation process (SREP) (EBA/GL/2014/13).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71882: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71884: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71885: 16.Proportionality in terms of the supervisory assessment of the NPE strategy of a SREP Category 3 or 4 institution can be achieved by aligning the assessment with the SREP engagement model, which ensures a risk-based approach to supervision and takes into account the systemic importance of the institution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71886: Addressees

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71887: 17. These guidelines are addressed to competent authorities as defined in point (i) of Article 4(2) of Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010. The guidelines are also addressed to credit institutions as defined in point 1 of Article 4(1) of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71888: Definitions

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71889: 18.Unless otherwise specified, terms used and defined in Directive 2013/36/EU, Regulation (EU) No 575/2013,12 and Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014, as amended and in force, have the same meaning in the guidelines.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71890: 19.In addition and in particular, for the purposes of these guidelines, the following definitions apply.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71891: Cure period

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71892: As defined in Part 2, paragraph 231(b), of Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71894: Earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortisation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71895: Forbearance

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71896: Forbearance measures as referred in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71897: Forborne exposures (FBEs)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71898: Exposures in respect to which forbearance measures have been applied in accordance with Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71899: Foreclosed assets

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71900: Assets obtained by taking possession of collateral and which remain recognised on the balance sheet. Foreclosed assets can be obtained through judicial procedures, through bilateral agreement with the borrower or through other types of collateral transfer from the borrower to the credit institution. Foreclosed assets may include financial and non-financial assets and should include all collateral obtained irrespective of accounting classification

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71901: Immovable property

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71902: Immovable property as defined in Article 208 of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71903: Liquidation cost

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71904: Liquidation costs are defined as the cash outflows incurred during collateral execution and the sales process and include:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:16]
PARAGRAPH_71905: 12 Regulation (EU) No 575/2013 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 26 June 2013 on prudential requirements for credit institutions and investment firms and amending Regulation (EU) No 648/2012 (OJ L 176, 27.6.2013, p. 1).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71907: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71909: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71910: a) all applicable legal costs; b) selling costs, taxes and other expenses; c) any additional maintenance costs to be incurred by the credit institution in relation to the repossession and disposal of the collateral; d) any cash inflows up to the date of liquidation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71911: Management body

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71912: As defined in points 7 and 8 of Article 3(1) of Directive 2013/36/EU

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71913: Movable property

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71914: Physical property other than immovable property in accordance with Article 210 of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71915: Non-performing exposures (NPEs)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71916: Exposures classified as non-performing in accordance with Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71917: Non-performing loans (NPLs)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71918: Loans and advances as defined in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014 that are classified as non-performing in accordance with Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71920: To calculate the NPL ratio, the gross carrying amount of NPLs and advances is divided by the gross carrying amount of total loans and advances in accordance with the NPE definition

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71921: NPE framework

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71922: Policies, processes, controls and systems for risk management of NPES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_71924: A group of exposures with similar credit risk characteristics

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71925: Probation period

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71926: As defined in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71927: Risk appetite framework (RAF)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71928: The overall approach, including policies, processes, controls and systems, through which risk appetite is established, communicated and monitored. It includes a risk appetite statement, risk limits and an outline of the roles and responsibilities of those overseeing the implementation and monitoring of the RAF. The RAF should consider material risks to the credit institution, as well as to its reputation with depositors, investors and customers. The RAF aligns with the bank's strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71929: Texas ratio

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:17]
PARAGRAPH_71930: Texas ratio: a ratio comparing the stock of NPLs with a credit institution's equity. NPLs (gross carrying amount) over equity and accumulated impairments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71932: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71934: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71935: 3. Implementation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71936: Date of application

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71937: 20.These guidelines apply from 30 June 2019.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71938: 21.For the first application of these guidelines, credit institutions should calculate their NPL ratios using the reference date of 31 December 2018.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71939: 4. NPE strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71940: 22. This section sets out the key elements for developing and implementing an NPE strategy. Credit institutions should have in place an adequate framework to identify, measure, manage, monitor and mitigate NPEs, including through workout activities.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71941: 23.In the development and implementation of their NPE strategies, credit institutions should take into account relevant consumer protection considerations and requirements, and ensure fair treatment of consumers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71942: 4.1 Developing the NPE strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71943: 24. Credit institutions should establish an NPE strategy to target a time-bound reduction of NPEs over a realistic but sufficiently ambitious time horizon (NPE reduction targets). The NPE strategy should lay out the credit institution's approach and objectives regarding effective management to maximise recoveries and ultimately a reduction in NPE stocks in a clear, credible and feasible manner for each relevant portfolio. When developing and implementing the NPE strategy for retail portfolios, credit institutions should consider provisions aimed at protecting consumers, including Directive 2014/17/EU, 13 Directive 2008/48/EC14 and the EBA Guidelines on arrears and foreclosure.15

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71944: 13 Directive 2014/17/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council of 4 February 2014 on credit agreements for consumers relating to residential immovable property and amending Directives 2008/48/EC and 2013/36/EU and Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010 (OJ L 60, 28.2.2014, p. 34).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71945: 14 Directive 2008/48/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 23 April 2008 on credit agreements for consumers and repealing Council Directive 87/102/EEC (OJ L 133, 22.5.2008, p. 66).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:18]
PARAGRAPH_71946: 15 Guidelines on arrears and foreclosure (EBA/GL/2015/12).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71948: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71950: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71951: 25. The following steps should form the core building blocks of the development and implementation of the NPE strategy:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71952: a) assessment of the operating environment and external conditions (see section 4.2);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71953: b) development of the NPE strategy over short-, medium- and long-term time horizons (see section 4.3);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71954: c) implementation of the operational plan (see section 4.4);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71955: d) fully embedding the NPE strategy into the management processes of the credit institution, including regular review and independent monitoring (see section 4.5).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71956: 26. When credit institutions develop their NPE strategy, they should also consider policies that aim to ensure the fair treatment of borrowers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71957: 4.2 Assessing the operating environment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71958: 27.As a first phase in the formulation and execution of an appropriate NPE strategy, credit institutions should complete an assessment of the following elements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71959: a) internal capabilities to effectively manage and reduce NPEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71960: b) external conditions and operating environment;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71961: c) the capital implications of the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71962: 4.2.1 Internal capabilities/self-assessment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71963: 28.Credit institutions should perform a comprehensive self-assessment to evaluate the actual situation and the steps to be taken internally to address any gaps in the internal capabilities to manage NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71964: 29.Institutions should fully understand and assess:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71965: a) The magnitude and drivers of their NPEs:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71966: i. the size and evolution of NPE portfolios at an appropriate level of granularity, which requires an appropriate grouping of the exposures, as outlined in section 5.2.3;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71967: ii. the drivers of NPE inflows and outflows, by portfolio where relevant;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71968: iii. other potential correlations and causations.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71969: b) The outcomes of NPE actions taken by the credit institution in the past:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:19]
PARAGRAPH_71970: i. the types and nature of actions implemented, including forbearance activities;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71972: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71974: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71975: ii. the effectiveness of those activities and related drivers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71976: c) Their operational capacities (processes, tools, data quality, IT/automation, staff/expertise, decision-making, internal policies and any other relevant area for the implementation of the strategy) in relation to the various steps involved in the process, including but not limited to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71977: i. early identification of NPEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71978: ii. forbearance activities;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71979: iii. impairments and write-offs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71980: iv. collateral valuations;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71981: V. recovery, legal process and foreclosure;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71982: vi. management of foreclosed assets, where relevant;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71983: vii. reporting and monitoring of NPEs and of the effectiveness of NPE workout solutions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71984: 30.Credit institutions should perform a comprehensive self-assessment covering at least the items listed in paragraph 29 on an annual basis to determine strengths, significant gaps and areas of improvement required to reach NPE reduction targets.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71985: 31.Credit institutions should report the outcome of the comprehensive self-assessment to the institution's management body and the competent authority.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71986: 32.Credit institutions should consider seeking expert views on their operational capabilities to manage NPEs from the institution's risk management and control functions or from external sources on a periodic basis.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71987: 4.2.2 External conditions and operating environment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71988: 33.Credit institutions should assess and consider the current and likely future external operating conditions and environment when establishing the NPE strategy and associated NPE reduction targets. The following list of external factors, where appropriate, should be taken into account by credit institutions when setting the NPE strategy:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71989: a) The macroeconomic conditions, including the dynamics of the real estate market or other relevant sectors, taking into account sector concentrations in NPE portfolios.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:20]
PARAGRAPH_71990: b) Market expectations with regard to acceptable NPE levels and coverage, including but not limited to the views of rating agencies and market analysts, and available research, taking proper account also of the interests of borrowers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71992: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_71994: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_71995: c) NPE investor demand, including trends in and the dynamics of the domestic and international NPE markets for portfolio sales.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_71996: d) The maturity of the NPE servicing industry and the availability and coverage of specialised servicers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_71997: e) The regulatory, legal and judicial framework. Credit institutions should have a good understanding of the legal proceedings related to NPE workout for different types of assets and different jurisdictions. In particular, credit institutions should assess the average duration of such proceedings, the average financial outcomes, the rankings of different types of exposures and related implications for outcomes, the influence of the types and rankings of collateral and guarantees on the outcomes, the impact of consumer protection issues on legal decisions, and the average total costs associated with legal proceedings. Legal provisions aimed at protecting consumers, in particular for residential mortgage exposures, should also be considered by credit institutions when setting the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_71998: f) The national tax implications of impairments and NPE write-offs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_71999: 4.2.3 Capital implications of the NPE strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72000: 34. Credit institutions should be able to calculate a detailed assessment of the impact of the planned strategy from capital, risk exposure amount, profit or loss, and impairment perspectives for each of the reduction drivers, and they should assess whether the bank has identified a strategic process to resolve any shortfalls under different economic scenarios. The assessment criteria, underlying assumptions and implications should be aligned with the RAF as well as with the internal capital adequacy assessment process (ICAAP).16

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72001: 35. Credit institutions should include suitable actions in their capital planning to ensure that the level of available capital will enable a sustainable reduction of NPEs on the balance sheet.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_72002: 4.3 Development of the NPE strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_72003: 36. The NPE strategy should encompass, at a minimum, time-bound quantitative NPE targets and foreclosed assets targets, supported, where appropriate, by a corresponding comprehensive operational plan. The development of the NPE strategy should be informed by a self- assessment process and an analysis of the strategic options for the implementation of the NPE strategy. The NPE strategy and operational plan should be defined and approved by the management body and reviewed at least annually.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_72004: 4.3.1 Strategy implementation options

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_72005: 37.Credit institutions should consider including a combination of strategies and options in the NPE strategy to achieve their objectives over the short, medium and long term. In order to

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:21]
PARAGRAPH_72006: 16 See Guidelines on ICAAP and ILAAP information collected for SREP purposes (EBA/GL/2016/10).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72008: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72010: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72011: successfully operationalise the NPE strategy, credit institutions should consider at least the following non-mutually exclusive implementation options for different portfolios and under different conditions:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72012: a) Hold/forbearance strategy: suitable workout strategy and forbearance options. The hold strategy option is strongly linked to the credit institution's operating model, forbearance and borrower assessment expertise, operational NPE management capabilities, outsourcing of servicing and write-off policies.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72013: b) Active portfolio reductions: sales, securitisation or, in the case of NPEs that are deemed unrecoverable, write-offs. This option is strongly linked to adequacy of impairments, collateral valuations, quality of exposure data and investors' demand for NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72014: c) Change of type of exposure or collateral, including foreclosure, debt to equity swapping, debt to asset swapping or collateral substitution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72015: d) Legal options: including insolvency proceedings or out-of-court solutions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72016: 38.Credit institutions should identify medium- and long-term strategy options for NPE reductions that may not be achievable immediately, for example due to a lack of immediate NPE investor demand, which might change in the medium to long term. The operational plan may therefore need to allow for such changes and require preparations for them, for example by enhancing the quality of NPE data in order to be ready for future investor transactions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72017: 39.When a credit institution concludes that none of the above options will lead to a sufficient NPE reduction in the medium to long term for certain portfolios or individual exposures, this should be clearly reflected in a timely impairment and write-off approach.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72018: 40.Credit institutions aiming to engage in complex processes, such as NPE risk transfer and securitisation transactions, should conduct robust risk analysis and have adequate risk control processes in place.17

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72019: 4.3.2 Targets

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72020: 41.Before commencing the short- to medium-term target-setting process, credit institutions should establish a view of reasonable long-term NPE levels, both at portfolio level and at aggregate level. Credit institutions should take into account historic or international benchmarks in order to define reasonable long-term NPE levels.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72021: 42.Credit institutions should include, at a minimum, clearly defined realistic yet ambitious quantitative targets in their NPE strategy, including for foreclosed assets, where relevant. These targets should lead to a concrete reduction, gross and net of impairments, in NPEs, at

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:22]
PARAGRAPH_72022: 17 As required for securitisation under Article 82(1) of Directive 2013/36/EU.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72024: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72026: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72027: least in the medium term. While expectations about changes in macroeconomic conditions, when based on solid external forecasts, can play a role in determining target levels, they should not be the sole driver of the NPE reduction targets established.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72028: 43.Credit institutions should establish targets as followings:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72029: a) by time horizons (short-term (indicative one year), medium-term (indicative three years) and possibly long-term);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72030: b) by main portfolios (e.g. retail mortgage, retail consumer, retail, small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs), corporate, large corporate, commercial real estate);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72031: c) by implementation options (e.g. cash recoveries from a hold strategy, collateral repossessions, recoveries from legal proceedings, revenues from sales of NPEs or write- offs).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72032: 44. The NPE targets for credit institutions should at a minimum include a projected absolute or relative NPE reduction, both gross and net of impairments, not only on an overall basis but also for the main NPE portfolios. Where foreclosed assets are material, a foreclosed assets strategy should be defined or, at least, foreclosed assets reduction targets should be included in the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72033: 45. The NPE targets should be aligned with the more granular operational targets. Further monitoring indicators can be implemented as additional targets, if deemed appropriate.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72034: 4.3.3 Operational plan

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72035: 46. The NPE strategy of the credit institution should be supported by an operational plan, which should be defined, approved and reviewed by the management body. The operational plan should clearly define how the credit institution will operationally implement its NPE strategy over a time horizon of at least one to three years (depending on the type of operational measures required).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72036: 47. The NPE operational plan should contain at least:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72037: a) clear time-bound objectives and goals;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72038: b) activities to be carried out on a portfolio basis;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72039: c) governance arrangements and structures, including responsibilities and reporting mechanisms for activities and outcomes;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72040: d) quality standards to ensure successful outcomes;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72041: e) staffing and resource requirements;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:23]
PARAGRAPH_72042: f) required technical infrastructure and an enhancement plan;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72044: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72046: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72047: g) granular and consolidated budget requirements for the implementation of the NPE strategy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72048: h) plans for communication with internal and external stakeholders (e.g. with regard to sales, servicing, efficiency initiatives).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72049: 48. The operational plan should have a specific focus on internal factors that could present impediments to the successful delivery of the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72050: 4.4 Implementing the operational plan

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72051: 49. The implementation of the NPE strategy operational plan should rely on suitable policies and procedures, clear ownership and appropriate governance structures, including escalation procedures, and the operational plan should incorporate wide-ranging change management measures in order to embed the NPE workout framework as a key element in the corporate culture.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72052: 50.Credit institutions should report material deviations from the plan to the management body and to the competent authority in a timely manner, with appropriate remediation actions to be put in place.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72053: 4.5 Embedding the NPE strategy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72054: 51.As the execution and delivery of the NPE strategy will involve and depend on many different areas within the credit institution, it should be embedded in processes at all levels of the organisation, including strategic and operational, including the risk committee as defined in Article 76(3) of Directive 2013/36/EU.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72055: 52.Credit institutions should emphasise to all relevant staff the key components of the NPE strategy in line with the approach taken to the institution's overall strategy and in particular the risk strategy as defined in Article 76 of Directive 2013/36/EU. This is especially important if the implementation of the NPE strategy will involve wide-ranging changes to business procedures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72056: 53.Credit institutions should clearly define and document the roles, responsibilities and formal reporting lines for the implementation of the NPE strategy and operational plan.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:24]
PARAGRAPH_72057: 54.Staff and management involved in NPE workout activities should be provided with clear individual (or team) goals and incentives geared towards reaching the targets agreed in the NPE strategy and operational plan. Related remuneration policies, career development objectives and performance monitoring frameworks should take the NPE targets into account in order to ensure the full engagement of staff and management with NPE reduction and should also have regard to the fair treatment of consumers. The incentive scheme for staff and managers in the loan origination/business units should also take into account the feedback from the workout activities and the quality of the credit institution's exposures in

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72059: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72061: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72062: order to disincentivise excessive risk taking. With regard to retail exposures, these remuneration policies should be developed in accordance with the EBA Guidelines on remuneration policies and practices related to the sale and provision of retail banking products and services.18

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72063: 55.All relevant components of the NPE strategy should be fully aligned with and integrated into the business plan and budget, including all the relevant costs associated with the implementation of the operational plan, and also potential losses stemming from NPE workout activities.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72064: 56. The NPE strategy should be fully embedded in the risk management framework. In that context, special attention should be paid to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72065: a) ICAAP:19 all relevant components of the NPE strategy should be fully aligned with and integrated into the ICAAP. Credit institutions should prepare quantitative and qualitative assessments of NPE developments under base and stressed conditions including the impact on capital planning.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72066: b) RAF:20 RAF and NPE strategies are closely interlinked. In this regard, there should be clearly defined RAF metrics and limits, approved by the management body, that are in alignment with the core elements and targets forming part of the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72067: c) Recovery plan:21 where NPE-related indicator levels and actions form part of the recovery plan, credit institutions should ensure that they are in alignment with the NPE strategy targets and operational plan.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72068: 57.Credit institutions should ensure a high level of monitoring and oversight by the risk management functions in respect of the formulation and implementation of the NPE strategy and operational plan.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72069: 18 Guidelines on remuneration policies and practices related to the sale and provision of retail banking products and services (EBA/GL/2016/06).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72070: 19 As defined in Article 108 of Directive 2013/36/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council of 26 June 2013 on access to the activity of credit institutions and the prudential supervision of credit institutions and investment firms (OJ L 176, 27.6.2013, p. 338).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72071: 20 As described in the Financial Stability Board's 'Principles for an effective risk appetite framework'.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:25]
PARAGRAPH_72072: 21 As required by Directive 2014/59/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council of 15 May 2014 establishing a framework for the recovery and resolution of credit institutions and investment firms and amending Council Directive 82/891/EEC, and Directives 2001/24/EC, 2002/47/EC, 2004/25/EC, 2005/56/EC, 2007/36/EC, 2011/35/EU, 2012/30/EU and 2013/36/EU, and Regulations (EU) No 1093/2010 and (EU) No 648/2012, of the European Parliament and of the Council (OJ L 173, 12.6.2014, p. 190).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72074: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72076: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72077: 5. NPE governance and operations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72078: 58.In order for credit institutions to be able to address their NPE issues in an efficient and sustainable manner, an appropriate governance structure and operational set-up should be in place.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72079: 59. This section sets out the key elements of governance and operations in relation to an NPE workout framework, covering aspects related to steering and decision-making, the NPE operating model, the internal control framework and NPE monitoring processes.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72080: 60.In the implementation of their NPE governance and operations, credit institutions should take into account relevant consumer protection considerations and requirements, and ensure fair treatment of consumers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72081: 5.1 Steering and decision-making

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72082: 61. The overarching strategy of a credit institution and its implementation should cover the NPE strategy and operational plan, which should therefore be set, approved and reviewed by the management body. In particular, the management body should:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72083: a) approve annually and regularly review the NPE strategy and operational plan in line with the overall risk strategy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72084: b) oversee the implementation of the NPE strategy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72085: c) define quantitative and qualitative management objectives and incentives for NPE workout activities;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72086: d) monitor on a quarterly basis progress made in comparison with the targets defined in the NPE strategy and operational plan;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72087: e) define adequate approval processes for NPE workout decisions (for large NPEs, these should involve the approval of the management body);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72088: f) approve NPE-related policies (including those listed in Annex 4) and processes, review them at least annually and proceed with any necessary amendments, ensuring that the policies and processes are completely understood by the staff;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72089: g) ensure sufficient internal controls on NPE management processes, with a special focus on activities linked to NPE classifications, impairments, write-offs, collateral valuations and the sustainability of forbearance solutions;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:26]
PARAGRAPH_72090: h) have sufficient knowledge, experience and expertise with regard to the management of NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72092: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72094: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72095: 62. The management body and senior management should dedicate an amount of their capacity and devote sufficient time to NPE workout-related matters in line with Article 76 of Directive 2013/36/EU, in proportion to the risks connected to NPEs within the credit institution. Credit institutions should establish and document clearly defined, efficient and consistent decision-making procedures, with adequate second line of defence involvement at all times.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72096: 5.2 NPE operating model

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72097: 5.2.1 NPE workout units

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72098: 63.In order to mitigate sufficiently any conflict of interest in managing NPEs, as well as to make good use of dedicated NPE expertise across the organisation, credit institutions should establish dedicated NPE workout units (NPE WUs) that are independent from loan origination activities. This separation of duties approach should encompass not only client relationship activities (e.g. negotiation of forbearance solutions with clients) but also the decision-making process. In this context, credit institutions should consider implementing dedicated decision- making bodies related to NPE workout (e.g. an NPE committee).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72099: 64. Where overlaps with the decision-making bodies, managers or experts involved in the loan origination process are unavoidable, the institutional framework and internal controls should ensure that any potential conflicts of interest are sufficiently mitigated.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72100: 65.Credit institutions should have arrangements in place to ensure that regular feedback between loan origination units and NPE WUs is established.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72101: 66. When designing an appropriate NPE WU structure, credit institutions should take into account the specificities of their main NPE portfolios, including the type of exposure (retail, SME, corporate) and the type of collateral.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72102: 67.Credit institutions should consider designing automated processes for NPE WUs for homogeneous retail NPE portfolios. For corporate NPE portfolios, where relevant, and depending on the sectoral concentration of the NPEs, credit institutions should consider a relationship management approach with sectoral specialisation of NPE WU staff. For sole traders and micro-enterprises, a combination of automated elements and a relationship management approach should be considered.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72103: 68.Smaller and less complex credit institutions (e.g. those that are classified in SREP Category 3 or 4) may have in place dedicated workout functions proportionate to their size, nature, complexity and risk profile. Credit institutions should ensure that the design of such functions prevents and eliminates conflict of interest in the management of NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:27]
PARAGRAPH_72104: 69.For proportionality purposes, smaller and less complex credit institutions (e.g. those that are classified in SREP Category 3 or 4), as an alternative to establishing dedicated decision-

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72106: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72108: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72109: making bodies related to NPE workout, may cover the necessary requirements in their existing credit or risk committees, as long as conflicts of interest are sufficiently mitigated.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72110: 5.2.2 Alignment with the NPE life cycle

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72111: 70.NPE WUs should be set up to ensure that NPE workout activities and borrower engagements are tailored to the phases of the NPE life cycle.22 Credit institutions should set up different NPE WUs for the different phases of the NPE life cycle and also for different portfolios, if appropriate. All applicable workout stages should receive adequate focus and should be equipped with sufficiently specialised staff.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72112: 71.Credit institutions should consider the following phases in the NPE life cycle, taking into account also the specificities of the products and the nature of the arrears:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72113: a) Early arrears (up to 90 days past due):23 during this phase, the focus should be on initial engagement with the borrower for early recoveries and on collecting information to enable a detailed assessment of the borrower's circumstances (e.g. financial position, status of loan documentation, status of collateral, level of cooperation, etc.). The type of exposure and collateral should ultimately determine the most suitable workout strategy, which may involve forbearance measures with a short-term time horizon, to be applied when necessary (including during this initial period, where appropriate), with the aim of stabilising the financial position of the borrower before establishing a suitable workout strategy. In addition, the credit institution should, where appropriate, seek options to improve its position while taking into account the rights and interests of consumers (e.g. by signing new loan documents, perfecting outstanding collateral, minimising cash leakage, taking additional collateral if available). A dedicated arrears management policy should contain guidance on the overall NPE workout procedures and responsibilities, including handover triggers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72114: b) Late arrears/forbearance: credit institutions should implement and formalise forbearance arrangements with borrowers in this phase. Forbearance arrangements should be put into place only where the credit institution is satisfied that the borrower can afford to make the repayments. In considering whether a restructuring option is viable, credit institutions should have regard to Article 28 of Directive 2014/17/EU24 and other legal provisions aimed at protecting consumers, to the extent applicable. A forbearance arrangement should be monitored for at least one year in line with Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014, given the increased risk, before it can eventually be transferred out of the NPE WUs if no further NPE triggers are observed.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72115: 22 This also encompasses assets not classified as NPEs - such as early arrears, FBEs and foreclosed assets - that play an essential role in the NPE workout process.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72116: 23 Unlikely to pay exposures could be part of either early arrears or NPE WUs, depending on their complexity.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:28]
PARAGRAPH_72117: 24 Directive 2014/17/EU of the European Parliament and of the Council of 4 February 2014 on credit agreements for consumers relating to residential immovable property and amending Directives 2008/48/EC and 2013/36/EU and Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010 (OJ L 60, 28.2.2014, p. 34).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72119: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_72120: EBA EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72121: c) Liquidation/debt recovery/legal cases/foreclosure: if no viable forbearance solution has been found due to the borrower's financial circumstances or cooperation level, credit institutions should perform a cost-benefit analysis of different liquidation options, including in-court and out-of-court procedures, having regard also to the interests of the borrower. Based on this analysis, credit institutions should speedily proceed with the chosen liquidation option, supported by legal and business liquidation expertise. Credit institutions that are engaged in extensive use of external experts should ensure that sufficient internal control mechanisms are in place to ensure an effective and efficient liquidation process. NPEs that have been categories as such for a long period of time should be given special attention in this regard. A dedicated debt recovery policy should contain guidance on liquidation procedures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_72122: 72.Managing foreclosed assets (or other assets stemming from NPEs): collateral repossession generally commences after other attempts by the credit institution to collect the outstanding amounts have failed. The credit institution should have a policy in place that describes the recovery process for foreclosed assets, covering in particular the steps of repossession, valuation of the collateral and realisation of various types of collateral through appropriate means.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_72123: 5.2.3 Grouping exposures

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72124: 73. The EBA Guidelines on credit risk management practices and accounting for expected credit losses25 describe the policies for credit institutions of grouping exposures with shared credit risk characteristics. Homogeneous portfolios should be built up in order to tailor treatments specifically to NPEs. Credit institutions should consider designing customised processes for each portfolio, with a dedicated expert team taking ownership of each. NPE portfolios should be analysed with a high degree of granularity, resulting in clearly defined borrower subportfolios. For these analyses, credit institutions should develop appropriate management information systems and sufficiently high data quality.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29]
PARAGRAPH_72125: 74.A list of potential selection criteria for grouping retail NPEs into portfolios is contained in Annex 1.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72126: 75.For corporate NPE portfolios, grouping by asset class or sector (e.g. commercial real estate, land and development, shipping, trading businesses) should be considered a key driver for NPE WU specialisation. These portfolios should then be further divided in line with the NPE strategy and the level of financial difficulty to ensure that workout activities are sufficiently focused.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:29] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72127: 25 Guidelines on credit institutions' credit risk management practices and accounting for expected credit losses (EBA/GL/2017/06).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72129: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72131: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72132: 5.2.4 Human resources

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72133: 76.Credit institutions should have in place an appropriate organisational framework relative to their business model and taking into account their risks, including risks stemming from NPEs. Credit institutions therefore should devote an appropriate and proportionate amount of management attention and resources to the workout of NPEs and to internal controls on related processes.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72134: 77.Sharing management and resources with other parts of the value chain (e.g. loan origination) should be carefully reviewed before implementation in order to avoid conflicts of interest and to ensure sufficient specialisation, as discussed above.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72135: 78.Based on the findings of the credit institution's NPE self-assessment on capabilities, as referred to in section 4.2.1, credit institutions should regularly review the adequacy of their internal and external NPE workout resources and address any human resourceng gaps in a timely fashion. As workout activities may place significant demands on resources, credit institutions should consider if it is appropriate to choose to use fixed-term contracts, internal/external outsourcing or joint ventures for NPE workout activities. However, the final responsibility for these activities remains with the credit institution. In the event that outsourcing is used, credit institutions should ensure that such outsourcing is arranged in accordance with the applicable legislation or regulatory requirements.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72136: 79.Credit institutions should build up the relevant expertise required for the defined NPE operating model, including the NPE WUs and internal control functions, in line with the provisions of the joint ESMA and EBA Guidelines on the assessment of the suitability of members of the management body and key function holders.26 Staff allocated to key NPE workout tasks should have specific NPE expertise and experience. Credit institutions should implement adequate and dedicated NPE training, including on consumer protection, and should design staff development plans to build in-house expertise using available talent.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72137: 80. Where it is not possible or efficient to build in-house expertise and infrastructure, the NPE WUs should have easy access to qualified independent external resources (e.g. property appraisers, legal advisors, business planners, industry experts) or to dedicated NPE servicing companies.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72138: 81. The credit institution, in alignment with the overall NPE strategy and operational plan, should implement an appraisal system tailored to the requirements of the NPE WUs. The appraisal system should be designed in line with the provisions of the EBA Guidelines on sound

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:30]
PARAGRAPH_72139: 26 Joint ESMA and EBA Guidelines on the assessment of the suitability of members of the management body and key function holders under Directive 2013/36/EU and Directive 2014/65/EU (EBA/GL/2017/12).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72141: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72142: EBA EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72143: remuneration policies 27 and Article 7 of Directive 2014/17/EU, 28 as well as for retail exposures, those of the EBA Guidelines on remuneration policies and practices related to the sale and provision of retail banking products and services.29 The appraisal system should be mainly linked to the quantitative elements of the credit institution's NPE targets but may also include qualitative elements (level of technical abilities relating to the analysis of financial information and data received, structuring of proposals, quality of recommendations or monitoring of restructured cases, as well as effective negotiation skills). The performance of the NPE WU staff should be regularly monitored and measured against these targets either on an individual basis or at team level, as appropriate.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72144: 82.The performance measurement framework for the management body and relevant managers should include specific indicators linked to the targets defined in the credit institution's NPE strategy and operational plan. The weights given to these indicators within the overall performance measurement framework should be proportionate to the severity of the NPE issues faced by the credit institution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72145: 83.Addressing early warnings signals and indicators should be encouraged by credit institutions through the remuneration policy and incentives framework in order to ensure that pre- arrears are efficiently addressed and NPE inflows thus effectively reduced.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72146: 5.2.5 Technical resources

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72147: 84.In terms of adequate technical infrastructure, credit institutions should ensure that all NPE- related data are centrally stored in robust and secure IT systems and that they are complete and up to date throughout the NPE workout process.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72148: 85.An adequate technical infrastructure should enable NPE WUs to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72149: a) Access all relevant data and documentation, including:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72150: i. current NPE and early arrears borrower information, including automated notifications;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72151: ii. exposure, collateral and guarantee information linked to the borrower or connected clients;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72152: iii. monitoring tools with the IT capabilities to track forbearance performance and effectiveness;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72153: 27 Guidelines on sound remuneration policies under Articles 74(3) and 75(2) of Directive 2013/36/EU and disclosures under Article 450 of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013 (EBA/GL/2015/22).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:31]
PARAGRAPH_72155: 29 Guidelines on remuneration policies and practices related to the sale and provision of retail banking products and services (EBA/GL/2016/06)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72159: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72160: iv. status of workout activities and borrower interaction, as well as details on forbearance measures agreed;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72161: V. foreclosed assets, where relevant;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72162: vi. tracked cash flow of the loan and collateral;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72163: vii. sources of underlying information and complete underlying documentation;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72165: b) Efficiently process and monitor NPE workout activities, including:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72166: i. automated workflows throughout the entire NPE life cycle;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72167: ii. an automated monitoring process for loan status, ensuring correct flagging of NPEs and FBEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72168: iii. incorporated warning signals;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72169: iv. automated quantitative reporting throughout the NPE workout life cycle as a basis for the analyses to be provided to NPE WU management, the management body and other relevant managers, as well as the regulator;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72171: vi. evolution monitoring of portfolios, subportfolios, cohorts and individual borrowers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72172: c) Define, analyse and measure NPEs and related borrowers:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72173: i. recognise NPEs and measure impairments;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72174: ii. perform suitable NPE portfolio analyses and store outcomes for each borrower;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72175: iii. support the assessment of the borrower's personal data, financial position and repayment ability, at least for non-complex borrowers;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:32]
PARAGRAPH_72176: iv. conduct calculations of (i) the net present value and (ii) the impact on the capital position of the credit institution for each restructuring option and/or any likely restructuring plan under any relevant legislation (e.g. foreclosure law, insolvency law) for each borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:33] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_72180: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_72181: 86. The adequacy of the technical infrastructure, including data quality, should be assessed by an independent internal or external audit function on a regular basis.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:33]
PARAGRAPH_72182: 5.3 Control framework

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:33]
