[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72478: 197. For prudential purposes, credit institutions should update valuations of all secured exposures in accordance with the requirements of Article 208(3) and Article 210(c) of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72479: 198. The group of collaterals that are subject to individual valuations and revaluations on a regular basis should be updated at the time when the exposure is classified as non- performing and at least annually while it continues to be classified as such. Credit institutions should make sure that, for the collateral subject to indexation or other similar methods, the indexation is updated at least annually.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72480: 199. For properties with an updated individual valuation that has taken place within the past 12 months (in line with all the applicable principles and requirements as set out in this section), the property value may be indexed up to the period of the impairment review.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72481: 200. Credit institutions should carry out more frequent monitoring where the market is subject to significant negative changes and/or where there are signs of significant decline in the value of the individual collateral.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72482: 201. Therefore, credit institutions should define criteria in their collateral valuation policy and procedures for determining if a significant decline in collateral value has taken place. Where possible, these will include quantitative thresholds for each type of collateral, based on the observed empirical data and any relevant qualitative credit institution experience, bearing in mind relevant factors such as market price trends or the opinion of independent appraisers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72483: 202. Credit institutions should have appropriate processes and systems in place to flag outdated valuations and to trigger valuation reports.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72484: 9.3 Valuation methodology

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72485: 9.3.1 General considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72486: 203. Credit institutions should have defined collateral valuation approaches for each collateral product type; these should be adequate and appropriate for the type of collateral in question.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53]
PARAGRAPH_72487: 204. All immovable property collateral should be valued on the basis of market value or mortgage lending value, as specified under Article 229 of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013. Movable property should be valued at its market value.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:53] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72488: 205. For movable property, credit institutions should, in accordance with the requirements of Article 199(6) of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013, periodically assess the liquidity of the property. If there is material volatility in the market prices, the institution should demonstrate that the valuation of the collateral is sufficiently conservative.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72490: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72492: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72493: 206. For movable property, credit institutions should, in accordance with the requirements of Article 210 of Regulation (EU) No 575/2013, conduct a sufficient legal review confirming the enforceability of the collateral, including an assessment of the legal right to enforce and liquidate the collateral in the event of default, within a reasonable timeframe.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72494: 207. Overall valuations based only on the discounted replacement cost should not be used. For income-generating properties, a market-comparable or discounted cash flow approach can be used.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72495: 208. Property collateral should be valued in accordance with applicable international, European and national standards.39

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72496: 9.3.2 Expected future cash flow

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72497: 209. Credit institutions should estimate discounted cash flow in a prudential manner and in line with applicable accounting standards.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72498: 210. Calculation of discounted cash flow should take into account cases where:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72499: a) the operating cash flow of the borrower continues and can be used to repay the financial debt, and collateral may be exercised to the extent that it does not influence operating cash flow; and

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72500: b) the operating cash flow of the borrower ceases and collateral is exercised.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72501: 211. When the estimation is based on the assumption that the operating cash flow of the borrower will continue, including cash flow being received from the collateral, updated and reliable information on cash flow is required.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72502: 212. When the estimation is based on the assumption that the operating cash flow of the borrower will cease, the future sale proceeds from collateral execution should be adjusted to take into account the appropriate liquidation costs and market price discount.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72503: 213. In addition to the above liquidation costs, a market price discount, if appropriate, should be applied to the updated valuation as outlined below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72504: 214. The property price at the time of liquidation should take into account current and expected market conditions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72505: 215. Time-to-sale considerations in connection with the disposal of mortgaged properties should also be included, based on debt enforcement practices and experiences from judicial proceedings at national level and on empirical evidence, and back-tested accordingly. These

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:54]
PARAGRAPH_72506: 39 These include the European Valuation Standards EVS-2016 (the Blue Book) and the Royal Institute of Chartered Surveyors (RICS) standards.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72508: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72510: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72511: considerations should include any operational costs or capital expenditures to be incurred before the time of sale.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72512: 216. The execution of collateral may include both consensual and non-consensual (forced) liquidation strategies.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72513: 217. The liquidation cost discount should reflect the manner of collateral execution, i.e. whether it is consensual or non-consensual.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72514: 218. The market price discount should reflect the liquidity of the market and the liquidation strategy. It should not reflect fire sale conditions unless the anticipated liquidation strategy actually involves a fire sale.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72515: 219. Credit institutions should apply adequate market price discounts for the purposes of IFRS 9, for the calculation of regulatory capital and for risk control purposes. A market price discount may be close to zero only for highly liquid and non-distressed collateral types that are not affected by any significant correlation risks.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72516: 220. All credit institutions should develop their own liquidation cost and market price discount assumptions based on observed empirical evidence. If insufficient empirical evidence is available, discount assumptions should be based on, at a minimum, liquidity, passage of time, and the quality/ageing of the appraisal. If a credit institution faces the situation of a frozen property market and only a small number of properties have been sold or the sales history has to be considered insufficient, a more conservative market price discount should apply.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55]
PARAGRAPH_72517: 9.4 Further considerations on estimating cash flow from property collateral liquidation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72518: 221. In estimating cash flow from property collateral liquidation, credit institutions should use appropriate and credible assumptions. In addition, credit institutions should pay attention to the requirements for valuing cash flow under IFRS 13 on fair value measurements. In particular, financial institutions should comply with the following requirements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72519: a) They must determine the assumed time of disposal taking into account current and expected market conditions as well as the underlying national legal framework regarding the disposal of mortgaged properties.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:55] [RISK:SYSTEMIC_RISK] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72520: b) They must ensure that the property price used to determine the estimated market value of property collateral at the point of liquidation is not based on macroeconomic projections/assumptions that are more optimistic than the projections produced by the relevant authorities and organisations such as International Monetary Fund (IMF) and the European System of Central Banks (ESCB)/ the European Systemic Risk Board (ESRB), and therefore does not assume an improvement on the current market conditions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72522: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72524: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72525: c) They must ensure that income from property collateral is not assumed to increase from the current levels unless there is an existing contractual arrangement for such an increase. Moreover, current income from property should be adjusted when calculating cash flow in order to reflect the expected economic conditions. Credit institutions should consider whether it is appropriate to project a flat income in a recessionary environment in which vacant properties are increasing and/or demand for transportation is decreasing, putting downwards pressure on income.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72526: d) A hold strategy on property collateral is not acceptable. A hold strategy is defined as holding the asset at above market value assuming that the asset will be sold after the market recovers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72527: 222. When using the value of collateral in assessing the recoverable amount of the exposure, at least the following should be documented:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72528: a) how the value was determined, including the use of appraisals, valuation assumptions and calculations;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72529: b) the supporting rationale for adjustments to appraised values, if any;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72530: c) the determination of selling costs, if applicable;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72531: d) the assumed timeline to recover;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72532: e) the expertise and independence of the appraiser.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72533: 223. When the observable market price is used to assess the recoverable amount of the exposure, the amount, source and date of the observable market price should also be documented.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72534: 224. Credit institutions should be able to substantiate the assumptions used when assessing the recoverable amount by providing to the competent authority, if requested, details on the property market value, the market price discount, legal and selling expenses applied, and the term used for the time to liquidation. Credit institutions should be able to fully justify their assumptions, both qualitatively and quantitatively, and explain the drivers of their expectations, taking past and current experience into account.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72535: 9.5 Back-testing

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:56]
PARAGRAPH_72536: 225. Credit institutions should demonstrate via sound back-testing that the assumptions used when assessing the recoverable amount were reasonable and grounded in observed experience. In this context, credit institutions should regularly back-test their valuation history (last valuation before the exposure was classified as non-performing) against their sales history (net sales price of collateral). Depending on the size and business model of the credit institution, it should differentiate by collateral type, valuation model/approach, type

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72538: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72539: EBA EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72540: of sale (voluntary/forced) and region for its back-testing process. The back-testing results should be used to determine haircuts on collateral valuations supporting exposures remaining on the balance sheet.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72541: 226. Alternatively, credit institutions using the advanced internal ratings based (A-IRB) approach may use secured loss given default (LGD) to determine haircuts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72542: 9.6 IT database requirements in respect of collateral

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72543: 227. Credit institutions should have databases of transactions to enable the proper assessment, monitoring and control of credit risk, to respond to requests from management and supervisors, and to enable the provision of information in periodic reports and other timely and comprehensive documentation. In particular, databases should comply with the following requirements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72544: a) sufficient depth and breadth, in that they cover all the significant risk factors;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72545: b) accuracy, integrity, reliability and timeliness of data;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72546: c) consistency - they should be based on common sources of information and uniform definitions of the concepts used for credit risk control;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72547: d) traceability, such that the source of information can be identified.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72548: 228. These databases should include all the relevant information on properties and other collateral for the credit institutions' transactions and on the links between collateral and specific transactions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72549: 9.7 Valuation of foreclosed assets

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72550: 229. Credit institutions should strongly consider classifying foreclosed assets as non-current assets held for sale under IFRS 5. This accounting treatment implies that the asset must be available for immediate sale in its present condition (IFRS 5.7), that the management body should approve an individual plan to sell the asset within a short timeframe (normally one year) and that an active sales policy should be pursued (IFRS 5.8); thus, it favours recoveries.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72551: 230. Foreclosed assets received should be valued at the lower of:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72552: a) the amount of the financial assets applied, treating the asset foreclosed or received in payment of debt as collateral;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72553: b) the fair value of the repossessed asset, less selling costs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:57]
PARAGRAPH_72554: 231. When fair value is not obtained by reference to an active market but is based on a valuation technique (either level 2 or level 3), some adjustments are necessary, in particular as a result of two factors:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72556: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_72558: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_72559: a) The condition or location of the assets. Risk and uncertainty regarding the asset should be incorporated in the fair value estimation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72560: b) The volume or level of activity of the markets in relation to these assets. The credit institution's previous experience of the entity in realisations and of the differences between amounts arrived at using the valuation technique and the final amounts obtained in realisations should be incorporated into the calculation. The assumptions made in order to measure this adjustment may be documented, and should be available to the supervisor on request. Illiquidity discounts may be considered.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_72561: 232. When credit institutions' foreclosed assets are still under construction and it is decided to complete construction before selling the asset, they should demonstrate the merits of such a strategy and the cost should not exceed the fair value less costs to complete and sell the asset taking into account an appropriate illiquidity discount as described above.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_72562: 233. When a foreclosed asset has exceeded the average holding period for similar assets for which active sales policies are in place, credit institutions should revise the illiquidity discount applied in the valuation process described above, increase it accordingly. In these circumstances, the credit institution should refrain from recognising write-backs/reversals of existing accumulated impairment on the asset, as its prolonged presence on the balance sheet provides evidence that the credit institution is unable to sell the asset at an increased valuation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:58]
PARAGRAPH_72563: 234. The frequency of valuation of foreclosed assets and the applicable procedures should follow the treatment of immovable property as set out in sections 9.1.2 and 9.2.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72565: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72567: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72568: 10. Supervisory evaluation of management of NPEs and FBEs

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72569: 235. As part of their ongoing engagement with credit institutions under the SREP, competent authorities should monitor the application of these guidelines by the credit institutions, in particular the development and implementation of NPE strategies and related governance and operational frameworks as described in sections 4 and 5. Competent authorities' assessments should include, but not be limited to, whether the credit institution's NPE strategy:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72570: a) is embedded into the credit institution's overall strategy and is subject to appropriate NPE governance, including a risk management and control framework;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72571: b) relies on a credible self-assessment of the credit institution's internal capabilities;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72572: c) adequately takes into account the credit institution's operating environment, external conditions and capital situation;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72573: d) covers not only a short-term time horizon but also a medium- and/or long-term time horizon;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72574: e) includes time-bound, realistic yet ambitious quantitative NPE targets and foreclosed assets targets where appropriate and is supported by an operational plan.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72575: 236. If the competent authority concludes that the NPE strategy of a credit institution clearly lacks one or more of the elements listed in points (a) to (e) of paragraph 235, it should be considered a serious shortcoming of the NPE strategy. In this case, competent authorities should require the immediate revision of the NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72576: 237. If the outcome of the competent authority's assessment is that the requirements of point (a) to (e) of paragraph 236 are broadly fulfilled by the NPE strategy, but some deficiencies are identified, the competent authority should ensure that credit institutions present an action plan on how to address the deficiencies and establish an effective and timely NPE management framework.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:59]
PARAGRAPH_72577: 238. Competent authorities should apply supervisory evaluation proportionately, taking into account the specificities of the institutions (e.g. in terms of size, nature and complexity). In their SREP assessments of NPE strategies and the supporting governance and operational arrangements, the competent authorities should consider also the business models of the institutions, in particular when the sole business of the institution is the purchase and sale of NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72579: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72581: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72582: 239. Proportionality in terms of the supervisory assessment of the NPE strategy of a smaller and less complex credit institution (e.g. an SREP Category 3 or 4 institution40) can be achieved by aligning the assessment with the SREP engagement model, which ensures a risk-based approach to supervision and takes into account the systemic importance of global and domestic institutions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72583: 240. Competent authorities should challenge credit institutions':

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72584: a) Operational plan and organisational arrangements if any of the following criteria is met:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72585: i. The framework for identifying, measuring, managing, monitoring and mitigating NPEs and FBEs, including for early recognition of NPEs and appropriate workout activities, is deemed inadequate by the competent authorities considering the size and complexity of the NPE problem at the credit institution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72586: ii. It does not allocate or does not foresee the future allocation of the necessary human and technical resources as well as providing for appropriate coverage by the internal control functions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72587: iii. It does not adequately describe the operationalisation of the monitoring process for NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72588: b) NPE strategy, if the combination of strategic options for the different portfolios and segments, including foreclosed assets, where applicable, does not result, in the authority's view, in the most effective and efficient strategy for NPE reduction.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72589: c) Capital plan, if it does not appropriately set out the planned reduction of NPEs from the balance sheet as per the NPE strategy and does not include suitable actions to ensure that a sufficient amount of capital and capital buffers are available, as well as envisaging timely and adequate impairments and write-offs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72590: d) Performance appraisal system, if the incentives for the management body and relevant managers and staff lack specific quantitative elements linked to the NPE reduction targets defined in the credit institution's NPE strategy.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72591: 241. Considering the importance of early detection and prevention of deteriorating credit quality, competent authorities should assess whether the early warning mechanisms are implemented in the credit institutions' internal procedures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72592: 242. Competent authorities should assess if credit institutions:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:60]
PARAGRAPH_72593: 40 Described in section 2.1.1, 'Categorisation of institutions', in the EBA Guidelines on SREP (EBA/GL/2014/13).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72595: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_72596: EBA EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72597: a) have in place a forbearance policy and related processes to assess the viability of forbearance measures and monitor the efficiency and effectiveness of forbearance measures;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_72598: b) recognise and classify NPEs and FBEs, including entry and exit criteria, consistently across the group and based on the definitions in Annex V to Commission Implementing Regulation (EU) No 680/2014;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61]
PARAGRAPH_72599: c) have in place policies and methodologies to ensure the measurement of impairments and write-offs for timely recognition of impairments and write-offs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72600: 243. Competent authorities should ensure that credit institutions have appropriate written policies and procedures in place regarding the valuation of property, as described in section 9. In particular, competent authorities should verify that these policies cover all immovable and movable property types that are used to secure credit exposures, the criteria for the application of individual versus indexed valuation and the requirements with regard to eligible appraisers.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72601: 244. If credit institutions report material deviations from the operational plan in accordance with section 4.4, competent authorities should assess whether the proposed remediation actions are sufficient to eliminate the deviation from the plan. The competent authority should require further actions of the credit institution if it is concerned about the effectiveness of the proposed actions.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:61] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72602: 245. The requirements set out above regarding the supervisory evaluation of the management of NPEs and FBEs supplement and further specify the assessment of NPEs and FBEs as part of credit risk management put forward in the EBA Guidelines on common procedures and methodologies for the SREP. The findings of this supervisory evaluation would feed into the assessment of credit risk under Title 6.2 of the EBA Guidelines on common procedures and methodologies for the SREP and would inform credit risk scores.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72604: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72606: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72607: Annex 1 - Sample criteria for grouping retail NPEs

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72608: 1. Natural or legal person:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72609: a) retail borrower

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72610: b) sole trader

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72611: c) small business or group of professionals

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72612: d) SME (overlaps with corporates).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72613: 2. Arrears bucket/days past due (dpd) (the higher the level of arrears the narrower the range of possible solutions):

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72614: a) early arrears (> 1 dpd and ≤ 90 dpd)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72615: b) late arrears (> 90 dpd and < 180 dpd)

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:62]
PARAGRAPH_72616: c) debt recovery unit (> 180 dpd, including also legal cases (borrowers in relation to whom legal actions have taken place or are in progress)).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72839: Annex 4 - Common NPE-related policies

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72840: Credit institutions should develop, regularly review and monitor their adherence to policies related to the NPE management framework.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72841: The following policies should be established, taking into account the principle of proportionality, aiming to achieve the implementation of the strategy of the credit institution (including its NPL strategy and operational plan where relevant).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72842: Arrears management policy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72843: This policy should set out the credit institution's NPE operating model (see section 5.2), including at least the following elements:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72844: . the structure and responsibilities of the NPE WUs, with clear handover triggers and a link to the grouping of exposures (see section 5.2.3);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72845: · the procedure to be followed by the functions involved, to include at a minimum:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72846: - the procedure and handover criteria to be followed for each stage of arrears, early arrears and late arrears;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72847: - the procedure to be followed where a borrower is classified as non-cooperating and/or non-viable, and the criteria for the borrower to be classified as such;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72848: - the communication with the borrower at each step, which should be aligned with the legislative framework of the country of operation (e.g. code of conduct);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72849: - monitoring tools and methods to be applied;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72850: · the human and technical resource requirements;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72851: . the reports to be produced internally for monitoring purposes and for regular updates to the management body.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72852: Credit institutions, when developing their arrears management policy, should take into account Article 28 of Directive 2014/17/EU and in particular the provisions of the EBA Guidelines on arrears and foreclosure.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72853: Forbearance policy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:71]
PARAGRAPH_72854: The forbearance policy described in section 6.2.1 should set out at least:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72856: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72858: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72859: . The necessary financial and non-financial documentation to be requested and provided by the different types of borrowers in order for the responsible credit officer to demonstrate repayment capacity on a principal and interest basis.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72860: . The minimum key financial repayment capacity metrics and ratios to be applied by the credit officer, detailed on a portfolio-/product-/sector-specific basis, in order to fully assess the borrower's repayment capacity; sector-specific guidelines for establishing key financial metrics and ratios on a sector-specific basis (SMEs and corporates).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72861: . The process for determining and implementing the most appropriate forbearance solution for a borrower:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72862: - For retail customers, decision trees are to be used. The process for retail customers should be in line with the provisions of the EBA Guidelines on arrears and foreclosure. For non-retail borrowers, if a decision tree approach is not appropriate, then the policy should provide clear instructions to the credit officer on how to assess the suitability of a forbearance treatment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72863: - In the case of borrowers for whom no solution can be reached (non-viable and/or non-cooperating borrowers), a time-bound process and procedure should be established for the transfer of these borrowers to the NPE WUs responsible for liquidation.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72864: . A toolkit of forbearance measures with short-term and long-term time horizons, as outlined in section 6.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72865: . Clear instructions to the credit officer regarding the requirements for revaluation of collateral in line with section 9.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72866: · The decision-making process, approval levels and procedures for each type of forbearance measure and size of exposure.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72867: . The process and procedure for the monitoring of the forbearance solutions granted and borrower performance following the completion of a restructuring, including frequency of the review of the borrower, the re-default definition, the process for reassessment and requirements for reporting of re-defaults.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72868: . The pricing policy for each forbearance measure and type of borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72869: Debt recovery/enforcement policy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:72]
PARAGRAPH_72870: The NPE WUs responsible for debt recovery should take the most appropriate actions in a timely manner to effectively reduce NPEs over a defined time horizon. The debt recovery policy, in accordance with the NPL strategy, should address, at a minimum:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72872: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72874: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72875: . The range of available options for each collateral type. Indicatively, the following could be considered (not in any particular order):

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72876: - voluntary asset sale (borrower re-engages and agrees to sell the asset);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72877: - forced asset sale via receivers/court proceedings (assets are not held on the balance sheet of the credit institution);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72878: - foreclosure of asset (assets are held on the balance sheet of the credit institution);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72879: - debt collection (internal or external);

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72880: - debt to asset/equity swap;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72881: - sale of loan/loan portfolio to a third party.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72882: . The procedure to be followed to select the most appropriate recovery option and the team of internal and external experts to be involved in taking the decision.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72883: . The recovery option should take into account the existence of collateral, type of legal documentation, type of borrower, local market conditions and macroeconomic outlook, the legislative framework in place, and potential historical recovery rates for each option versus the costs involved for each option.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72884: · A clear definition of non-cooperating borrowers or a link to related policies including such a definition.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72885: . A clearly defined approval process for each stage of the debt recovery process for the different recovery options available to the credit institution.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72886: . The role of risk control and internal audit departments in the procedure and in the monitoring process.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72887: With respect to the liquidation of collateral, the following should be defined in the policy:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72888: · The valuation approach to be followed in respect of the asset (in line with section 9.7) including the liquidation costs to be applied. The liquidation costs should be in line with requirements set out in section 9.3.3

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73]
PARAGRAPH_72889: · Involvement of internal or external experts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:73] [RISK:CONCENTRATION_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72891: - to the amount of assets that can be held by the credit institution at any point of time, taking into account the large exposure limits specified in the CRD and industry concentration risk, for example in the real estate sector;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72893: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72895: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72896: - to the amount of repossessed or foreclosed assets that can be acquired by the credit institution within a certain time period.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72897: . The procedure to be followed post repossession or foreclosure to develop and implement a sale strategy, and the unit within the credit institution responsible for undertaking the management of the assets concerned (this may also be defined in a separate foreclosed/repossessed asset policy).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72898: Credit institutions should consider the interaction with other creditors for NPE borrowers with multiple creditors, usually corporate borrowers. Therefore, credit institutions should put in place a clear procedure for negotiating and interacting with other financial institutions (or other third parties) to whom the borrower is indebted.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72899: Collateral policies

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74] [RISK:CREDIT_RISK]
PARAGRAPH_72900: Given the importance of credit risk mitigation in the NPE workout process, credit institutions should develop clear and consistent collateral policies, including policies for foreclosed assets. These policies should comprehensively cover the management, valuation and reporting of all collateral types. Given the complexity and specialisation of some types of collateral, credit institutions should seek external expertise in drafting and reviewing these policies. Credit institutions should ensure a consistent approach to managing and valuing similar collateral across the portfolio, as per section 9.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72901: NPE monitoring policy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72902: A dedicated policy should be established specifying, inter alia:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72903: · the types of actions required in response to the different types of findings;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72904: · escalation procedures;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72905: · key elements, frequency and recipients of the reporting;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72906: · handover criteria/a link to NPL procedures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72907: Outsourcing/NPL servicing policy

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:74]
PARAGRAPH_72908: A dedicated policy should be established for the outsourcing of services to third parties if this is relevant. This needs to include the required procedures for the selection of outsourcing partners, the required legal contract content and the decision-making process for outsourcing agreements, as well as the monitoring of those agreements.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72910: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72912: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72913: Annex 5 - Possible forbearance measures

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72914: Forbearance measure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72915: Description

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72916: Viability and other important considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72917: 1. Interest only

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72918: During a defined short-term period, only interest is paid on credit facilities and no principal repayment is made. The principal amount thus remains unchanged and the terms for the repayment structure are reassessed at the end of the interest-only period, subject to the assessed repayment ability.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72919: This measure should be considered viable only if the credit institution can demonstrate (based on reasonable documented financial information) that the financial difficulties experienced by the borrower are of a temporary nature and that after the defined interest-only period the borrower will be able to service the loan at least to the extent of the previous repayment ability. The measure should generally not exceed a period of 24 months and, in the case of construction of commercial property and project finance, 12 months. Once the defined period of this forbearance measure is over, institutions should reassess the borrower's debt- servicing capacity in order to proceed with a revised repayment schedule that is able to account for the unpaid capital element during this interest-only period. In most cases, this measure will be offered in combination with other measures of a longer-term nature to compensate for the temporary lower repayments (e.g. extension of maturity).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72920: 2. Reduced payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72921: Decrease in the amount of repayment instalments over a defined short-term period in order to accommodate the borrower's affected cash flow situation, before continuing with the repayments on the basis of projected repayment ability. The interest remains to be paid in full.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72922: See '1. Interest only'. If the amount of the payment reduction is moderate and all other conditions mentioned above are met, this measure could be applied for a period longer than 24 months.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72923: 3. Grace period/payment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72924: An agreement allowing the
borrower a defined delay in fulfilling the repayment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72925: See '1. Interest only.'

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:75]
PARAGRAPH_72926: moratorium

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72928: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72930: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72931: Forbearance measure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72932: Description

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72933: Viability and other important considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72934: obligations, usually with regard to the principal and interest.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72935: 4. Arrears/interest capitalisation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72936: Forbearance of arrears and/or accrued interest arrears by the addition of those unpaid amounts to the outstanding principal balance for repayment under a sustainable rescheduled programme.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72937: The measure should be granted/considered viable only where the institution has assessed that the borrower's verified income/expenditure levels (based on reasonable documented financial information) and the proposed revised repayments are sufficient to enable the borrower to service the revised loan repayment on a principal and interest basis for the duration of the revised repayment schedule, and where the institution has formally sought confirmation that the borrower understands and accepts the capitalisation conditions. Arrears capitalisation should be provided only selectively in cases where the recovery of historical arrears or payments due under the contract is not possible and capitalisation is the only option realistically available. Institutions should generally avoid offering this measure to a borrower more than once, and the measure should be applied only to arrears that do not exceed a predefined size relative to the overall principal (which should be defined in the credit institution's forbearance policy). The institution should assess the percentage of arrears being capitalised compared with the principal and interest repayments as adequate and appropriate for the borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72938: 5. Interest rate reduction

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72939: Permanent (or temporary) reduction in interest rate (fixed or variable) to a fair and sustainable rate.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:76]
PARAGRAPH_72940: Exposures with high interest rates are one of the common causes of financial distress. The financial difficulties of a borrower may partly derive from the fact that the interest rates are excessively high compared with the income of the borrower or from the fact that the evolution of interest rates, as opposed to a fixed rate, has resulted in the borrower receiving finance at an exorbitant cost, compared with prevailing market conditions. In such cases, an interest rate reduction could be considered.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72942: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72944: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72945: Forbearance measure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72946: Description

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72947: Viability and other important considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72948: If affordability can be achieved only at below-risk or below- cost rates, this should be clearly flagged.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72949: This measure could be applied also as a short-term measure.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72950: 6. Extension of maturity/term

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72951: Extension of the maturity of the loan (i.e. of the last contractual loan instalment date), which allows a reduction in instalment amounts by spreading the repayments over a longer period.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72952: If the borrower is subject to a compulsory retirement age, term extension should be considered viable only where the institution has assessed and can demonstrate that the borrower can, through a pension or other sources of verified income, service the revised loan repayments on an affordable basis. Term extension should be considered viable only where it is in line with the life cycle of existing collaterals or proper substitution of the existing collaterals occurs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72953: 7. Additional collateral

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72954: Additional liens on unencumbered assets are obtained as additional collateral from the borrower in order to compensate for the higher risk exposure and as part of the restructuring process.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72955: This measure is not a viable standalone forbearance measure as it does not in itself resolve the presence of arrears on a loan. It usually aims to improve or cure LTV ratio covenants. Additional collateral may take many forms, such as a pledge on a cash deposit, assignment of receivables or a new/additional mortgage on immovable property.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72956: Institutions should value second and third liens on assets as well as personal guarantees with care.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72957: 8. Sale by agreement/assisted sale

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72958: The credit institution and the borrower agree to voluntarily dispose of the secured asset(s) to partially or fully repay the debt.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72959: Credit institutions should restructure any residual debt post the assisted sale with an appropriate repayment schedule in line with the borrower's reassessed repayment ability.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72960: For forbearance measures that may require the sale of the property at the end of the term, credit institutions should conservatively consider the future approach to any shortfall that could remain after the sale of the property and address it as early as possible.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:77]
PARAGRAPH_72961: For exposures that are repaid by repossession of collateral at a predefined moment, the repossession does not

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72963: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72965: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72966: Forbearance measure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72967: Description

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72968: Viability and other important considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72969: constitute a forbearance measure unless it is exercised ahead of the predefined moment due to financial difficulties.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72970: 9. Rescheduled payments

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72971: The existing contractual repayment schedule is adjusted to a new sustainable repayment programme based on a credible, current and forecasted assessment of the borrower's cash flow

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72972: Different repayment options may include: i. Partial repayment: when a payment is made against the exposure, for example from a sale of assets that is lower than the outstanding balance. This option is applied to significantly reduce the exposure at risk and to enable a sustainable repayment programme for the remaining outstanding amount. This option should be preferred to the bullet and step-up options described below.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72973: ii. Balloon or bullet payments: when the rescheduled repayment ensures a large payment of the principal at a later date before loan maturity. This option should be used/considered viable only in exceptional circumstances and when the institution can duly demonstrate future cash flow availability by the borrower to meet the balloon or bullet payment.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72974: iii. Step-up payments: credit institutions should consider a solution including this option viable only when they can ensure, and are able to demonstrate, that there is good reason to expect that future increases in payments can be met by the borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72975: 10. Conversion of currency

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72976: When the currency of the exposure is aligned with the currency of the cash flow.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72977: Credit institutions should explain fully to borrowers the risks of foreign exchange and should also refer to currency conversion insurance.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72978: 11. Other alteration of contract conditions/covenants

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72979: When the credit institution discharges the borrower of covenants or conditions included in a loan agreement not listed above.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72980: 12. Refinancing/new credit facilities

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78]
PARAGRAPH_72981: Providing new financing
arrangements in order to
support the recovery of a
distressed borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:78] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72982: This is usually not a viable standalone
forbearance measure; it should be
combined with other forbearance
measures addressing existing arrears. It should be applied only in exceptional cases.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72984: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72986: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72987: Forbearance measure

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72988: Description

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72989: Viability and other important considerations

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72990: New credit facilities may be granted that may entail the pledging of additional collateral. In the case of inter-creditor arrangements, the introduction of covenants may be necessary to compensate for the additional risk incurred by the credit institution. This measure may be more suitable for corporate exposures; a thorough assessment of the borrower's ability to pay should be performed, including sufficient involvement of independent sectoral experts to judge the viability of business plans and cash flow projections provided. This measure should be considered viable only when the thorough affordability assessment demonstrates repayment capacity in full.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72991: 13. Debt consolidation

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72992: Combining multiple exposures into a single exposure or a limited number of exposures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72993: This is usually not a viable standalone forbearance measure; it should be combined with other forbearance measures addressing existing arrears. This measure is particularly beneficial in situations where combining collateral and secured cash flow provides greater overall collateral coverage for the entire debt, for example, by minimising cash leaks or by facilitating reallocation of cash flow surplus between exposures.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72994: 14. Partial or total debt forgiveness

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79]
PARAGRAPH_72995: The credit institution forfeits the right to legally recover part or the whole of the amount of the debt outstanding from the borrower.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:79] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72996: This measure should be used where the credit institution agrees to a 'reduced payment in full and final settlement' whereby the credit institution will forgive all of the remaining debt if the borrower repays the reduced amount of the principal balance within an agreed timeframe. Credit institutions should apply debt forgiveness options carefully, since the possibility of forgiveness can give rise to moral hazard and thus might encourage 'strategic defaults'. Therefore, institutions should define specific forgiveness policies and procedures to ensure strong controls are in place.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_72998: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73000: EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73001: Accompanying documents

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73002: Impact assessment

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73003: The 'Council conclusions on Action plan to tackle NPLs in Europe' require the EBA to issue, by summer 2018, general guidelines on NPL management and internal governance, consistent with the Single Supervisory Mechanism (SSM) guidance for significant institutions, i.e. its 'Guidance to banks on Non-Performing Loans' (SSM guidance).41 More precisely, the Council requests that one of the (preferred) policy options presented in the Report of the Financial Services Committee (FSC) Subgroup on Non-Performing Loans.42 As a result, this section uses the latter as a baseline for the analysis.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73004: As per Article 16(2) of the EBA Regulation (Regulation (EU) No 1093/2010 of the European Parliament and of the Council), any guidelines developed by the EBA must be accompanied by an impact assessment (IA) that analyses 'the potential related costs and benefits'. This IA must provide the reader with an overview of the findings as regards the problem identification, the options identified to remove the problem and their potential impacts.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73005: This annex presents the IA with a cost-benefit analysis of the provisions included in the guidelines put forward in this Consultation Paper. Given the nature of the study, the IA is high level and qualitative in nature.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73006: A. Problem identification

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73007: The main (specific) problem that the current guidelines aim to address is the limitations on the scope of implementation of the SSM guidance. The SSM guidance covers a set of microprudential measures and supervisory tools for monitoring and assessing the performance of significant institutions under the SSM's direct supervision regarding their strategy, governance and operations in relation to NPL management. In other words, the current scope of the policy implementation on NPL management is limited to significant institutions (and to their national, European and international subsidiaries) and does not cover other (less significant) institutions and banks outside the Banking Union. Yet there may be some other banks that are not subject to the SSM guidance that continue to have high levels of NPLs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73008: Overall, the exclusion of the banks that fall outside the scope of the SSM's direct supervision from NPE management rules prevents the achievement of the ultimate policy objectives of tackling the high NPE levels in the EU.43 This could lead to:

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80]
PARAGRAPH_73009: 41 Press Release 459/17 (11/07/2017).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73010: 42 Report of the FSC Subgroup on Non-Performing Loans (9854/17); see 'Policy Option A.1' (p. 55).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:80] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73011: Report of the FSC Subgroup on Non-Performing Loans (9854/17); see 'Policy Option A.1' (p. 55).

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73013: FINAL REPORT - GUIDELINES ON MANAGEMENT OF NON-PERFORMING AND FORBORNE EXPOSURES

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73014: EBA EUROPEAN BANKING AUTHORITY

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73015: " a lack of necessary monitoring and assessment tools to enable supervisors to oversee the management of NPEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73016: " a lack of timely recognition and intervention to tackle problems related to high levels of NPEs;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73017: " obstacles to achieving supervisory convergence in the treatment of NPLs and to implementing a proactive NPE management strategy;

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73018: " obstacles to fostering and monitoring sound credit management and internal governance to prevent the emergence of excessive levels of NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73019: The current practice not only leaves a large number of EU banks outside the scope of NPE monitoring and assessment but may also have a negative effect on the level-playing field and supervisory convergence in the EU banking sector.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73020: B. Policy objectives

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73021: The general objectives of the guidelines are to (i) provide supervisors with the necessary and effective tools to oversee the management of NPEs by banks and ensure their timely recognition and provisioning, (ii) promote supervisory convergence in the treatment of NPEs across EU banks, (iii) ensure that all relevant high NPE banks implement a proactive NPL management strategy, and (iv) foster and monitor sound credit originating standards, risk management and internal governance, to prevent the (re-)emergence of excessive levels of NPEs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73022: The specific objective of the guidelines for these purposes is to extend the scope of the supervisory monitoring and assessment of banks' NPE management to the entire EU banking sector to (i) ensure an effective supervisory framework to tackle NPE-related problems, (ii) promote supervisory convergence across EU banks and (iii) ensure a level-playing field in the EU banking sector.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73023: C. Baseline scenario

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81] [REQ_TYPE:MANDATORY]
PARAGRAPH_73024: In March 2017, the SSM adopted its 'Guidance to banks on Non-Performing Loans'. The objective of the SSM guidance is for banks to define and implement quantitative policies and targets to address high levels of NPLs.

[JURISDICTION:FINNISH] [SOURCE:EBA] [CATEGORY:FINANCIAL_REGULATION] [PAGE:81]
PARAGRAPH_73025: A total of 119 banks fall within the scope of the SSM guidance; the current rules do not cover over 6 000 other institutions that are operating in the EU. Furthermore, significant banks are mostly large banks that have relatively low levels of NPL/NPE ratios, while medium and small banks, in terms of their volume of total assets and level of cross-border activities, on average, have higher levels of NPL/NPE ratios. The EBA collects supervisory data from a sample of EU banks.44 These
